posted:Posted July 1, 2023
msg:First of all, let me make a conclusion. The actual staying experience in this hotel can be said to be the worst in recent years.

Letâ€™s talk about the most serious problem first: entering and exiting our room without permission and using our room as a utility room to display miscellaneous items. The cause was that the toilet in the room had a small amount of water, which caused the toilet to be blocked when I went to the toilet at two o'clock in the middle of the night. I called the staff to repair it, but to no avail. We had to change rooms because dirty water was pouring onto the floor. At that time, all our luggage was still spread out in the room, and the staff who repaired the toilet promised that we would not enter the room and touch our things before we checked out. As a result, when I returned to the original room the next morning, I found that it was filled with miscellaneous bed sheets and quilt covers, and my luggage had been moved. After I reported the issue to the so-called housekeeper, two people from the guest house tried to get into our room. Moreover, at first the housekeeping depar**ent argued that they had not touched our things, but they only admitted that they had been moved when we were facing the line in the room. Let me ask you: before we checked out, why did the staff come in and out of our room at will like visiting a vegetable market? Are you so blind to the privacy of hotel guests?

Letâ€™s talk about all the bad things that almost broke the camelâ€™s back. In the room I stayed in at the beginning, the water flow from the sink faucet was so small that it took a century to wash my hands. The temperature of the water in the shower room could not be adjusted, and I experienced the feeling of being afraid of boiling water even if I was a dead pig. The room I changed later became more mysterious. When I slept until early in the morning, the TV suddenly turned on by itself. I searched for the remote control for a long time but couldn't find it. I had to get up sleepily and struggle to turn off the power on the TV. After I went to the toilet, the smart phone turned on. After about ten minutes, the toilet started to water on its own. The so-called intelligence is more like ****. In fact, even if it is equipped with an ordinary toilet, so many outrageous things will not happen.

Finally, to be objective and fair, Manager Zhang Xiyao, who later came forward to handle the complaint, had a very good attitude. She did not try to make any unnecessary excuses, and gave us sincere compensation measures: a full refund of the one-night room fee, and drove us there in person. We were sent to the boarding point of the Great Falls Scenic Area, which saved a lot of time on the road, and they also took the initiative to provide us with a lunch. If all the staff at the B&B could show such a professional attitude towards guests and handle problems, there wouldn't be so much unpleasantness.

Everyone came out to have fun and have fun. This may be the only time in this life that we come to Huangguoshu. It is really a pity to leave such a bad impression. All good and bad experiences have been stated truthfully. I hope the B&B can continue to strengthen personnel management and service awareness!
